        <section id="introduction">
         <!--Title-->
         <h2 class="primary-heading">
          Datatables
         </h2>
         <h1 class="secondary-heading mb-4">
          Bootstrap 4 datatables integration
         </h1>
         <!--Description-->
         <p>
          MDBootstrap integration with a very popular plugin enhances the possibilities of standard tables.
         </p>
         <blockquote class="blockquote bq-primary">
          <p class="bq-title">
           To start working with DataTables, please see the
           <strong>
            "Getting Started"
           </strong>
           tab on this page.
          </p>
          <p>
           <strong>
            Note:
           </strong>
           Datatables integration is available from version
           <strong>
            4.5.7
           </strong>
           (released on 16.07.2018).
          </p>
         </blockquote>
         <blockquote class="blockquote bq-danger">
          <p class="bq-title">
           New version of Datatables
          </p>
          <p>
           This documentation may contain syntax introduced in the
           <strong>
            MDB 4.16.0
           </strong>
           and can be incompatible with previous versions. For old datatables documentation please follow the
           <a href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/datatables1/">
            link
           </a>
           .
          </p>
         </blockquote>
        </section>

         <p>
          To use DataTables call the
          <code>
           $().DataTable()
          </code>
          method on the table. An example is given in the
          <strong>
           "JavaScript"
          </strong>
          tab in
    the code below.

<section id="material-design-example">
 <!--Title-->
 <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
  Material Design example
  <a class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/products/jquery-ui-kit/" role="button" target="_blank">

   </i>

<div class="tab-pane fade" id="mdb_61d52f465268b45ad4ce75055b30afc8" role="tabpanel">
 <pre class="grey lighten-3 px-3 mb-0 line-numbers language-js" data-editor="false"><code>

        // Material Design example
        $(document).ready(function () {
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample').DataTable();
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper').find('label').each(function () {
            $(this).parent().append($(this).children());
          });
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_filter').find('input').each(function () {
            const $this = $(this);
            $this.attr("placeholder", "Search");
            $this.removeClass('form-control-sm');
          });
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_length').addClass('d-flex flex-row');
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_filter').addClass('md-form');
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper select').removeClass('custom-select custom-select-sm form-control form-control-sm');
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper select').addClass('mdb-select');
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .mdb-select').materialSelect();
          $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_filter').find('label').remove();
        });

      </code></pre>

<hr class="my-5"/>
<!--Section: -->
<section id="select">
 <!--Title-->
 <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
  DataTable with select
 </h2>
 <!-- Description -->
 <p>
  With our DataTable component, you can use DataTable select.
 </p>
 <p>
  You have to include the path to a DataTable, then select CSS and JavaScript. The files are located in the
  <code>
   addons
  </code>
  folder.
 </p>
 <!--Section: Code-->
 <section>
  <!-- mdbsnippet -->
  <div class="docs-pills">
   <div class="d-flex justify-content-between">
    <ul class="nav md-pills pills-grey">

<section id="multi-checkbox-example">
 <!--Title-->
 <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
  DataTable multi checkbox example
 </h2>
 <!-- Description -->

<div class="tab-pane fade" id="mdb_57bb970851d918ace2b71bc5aa1963e7" role="tabpanel">
 <pre class="grey lighten-3 px-3 mb-0 line-numbers language-js"><code>

        $(document).ready(function () {
          $('#dt-filter-select').dataTable({

            initComplete: function () {
              this.api().columns().every( function () {
                  var column = this;
                  var select = $('&lt;select  class="browser-default custom-select form-control-sm"&gt;&lt;option value="" selected&gt;Search&lt;/option&gt;&lt;/select&gt;')
                      .appendTo( $(column.footer()).empty() )
                      .on( 'change', function () {
                          var val = $.fn.dataTable.util.escapeRegex(
                              $(this).val()
                          );
        
                          column
                              .search( val ? '^'+val+'$' : '', true, false )
                              .draw();
                      } );
        
                  column.data().unique().sort().each( function ( d, j ) {
                      select.append( '&lt;option value="'+d+'"&gt;'+d+'&lt;/option&gt;' )
                  } );
              } );
          }
          });
        });


      </code></pre>
</div>

<div class="tab-pane fade" id="mdb_472ba255f170c22a766f08d60d9f9558" role="tabpanel">
 <pre class="grey lighten-3 px-3 mb-0 line-numbers language-js"><code>

        $(document).ready(function () {
          $('#dt-filter-search').dataTable({
    
            initComplete: function () {
              this.api().columns().every( function () {
                  var column = this;
                  var search = $(`&lt;input class="form-control form-control-sm" type="text" placeholder="Search"&gt;`)
                      .appendTo( $(column.footer()).empty() )
                      .on( 'change input', function () {
                          var val = $(this).val()
        
                          column
                              .search( val ? val : '', true, false )
                              .draw();
                      } );
        
              } );
          }
          });
        });


      </code></pre>

        $(document).ready(function () {
          $('#dt-bordered').dataTable({

            columnDefs: [{
              orderable: false,
              className: 'select-checkbox',
              targets: 0
            }],
            select: {

<section id="otpions-reference">
 <!--Title-->
 <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
  Options reference
 </h2>
 <!-- Table  -->
 <table class="table table-hover table-sm table">
  <!-- Table head -->
  <thead>
   <tr>
    <th>
     #
    </th>
    <th>
     Name
    </th>
    <th>
     Description
    </th>
   </tr>
  </thead>
  <!-- Table head -->
  <!-- Table body -->
  <tbody>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     1
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      autoWidth
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Feature controlling DataTables' smart column width handling
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     2
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      info
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Feature controlling the table information display field
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     3
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      ordering
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Feature controlling the ordering (sorting) abilities in DataTables.
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     4
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      paging
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Enable or disable table pagination.
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     5
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      scrollX
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Horizontal scrolling
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     6
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      scrollY
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Vertical scrolling
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     7
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      searching
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Feature control the search (filtering) abilities
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     8
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      order
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Cell
    </td>
   </tr>
   <tr>
    <th scope="row">
     9
    </th>
    <td>
     <code>
      order
     </code>
    </td>
    <td>
     Initial order (sort) to apply to the table
    </td>
   </tr>
  </tbody>
  <!-- Table body -->
 </table>

<section id="advanced-table-options">
 <!--Title-->
 <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
  Advanced table options
 </h2>
 <!-- Description -->
 <p>
  For advanced table options, take a look at the specific documentation pages listed below.
 </p>
 <!-- List group -->
 <div class="list-group">
  <!-- Item -->
  <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/additional/" target="_blank">
   <div>
    <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
     <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
      Tables with additional elements and customization options
     </h5>
    </div>
    <p class="mb-1">
     Tables with buttons, checkboxes, icons, panels &amp; more.
    </p>
   </div>
   <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
   </i>
  </a>
  <!-- Item -->
  <!-- Item -->
  <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/responsive/" target="_blank">
   <div>
    <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
     <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
      Table responsive
     </h5>
    </div>
    <p class="mb-1">
     Advanced options for responsive tables
    </p>
   </div>
   <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
   </i>
  </a>
  <!-- Item -->
  <!-- Item -->
  <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/pagination/" target="_blank">
   <div>
    <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
     <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
      Table pagination
     </h5>
    </div>
    <p class="mb-1">
     Pagination is a simple navigation method that lets you split a huge amount of content within a
          table into smaller parts.
    </p>
   </div>
   <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
   </i>
  </a>
  <!-- Item -->
  <!-- Item -->
  <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/search/" target="_blank">
   <div>
    <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
     <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
      Table search
     </h5>
    </div>
    <p class="mb-1">
     The MDBootstrap search box enables super-fast searching among all the table data.
    </p>
   </div>
   <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
   </i>
  </a>
  <!-- Item -->
 </div>
 <!-- List group -->
 <!-- Item -->
 <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/sort/" target="_blank">
  <div>
   <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
    <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
     Table sort
    </h5>
   </div>
   <p class="mb-1">
    This functionality lets you sort the data in the tables according to any specific columns.
   </p>
  </div>
  <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
  </i>
 </a>
 <!-- Item -->
 <!-- Item -->
 <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/scroll/" target="_blank">
  <div>
   <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
    <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
     Table scroll
    </h5>
   </div>
   <p class="mb-1">
    If your table is too long or too wide you can limit its size and enable scroll functionality.
   </p>
  </div>
  <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
  </i>
 </a>
 <!-- Item -->
 <!-- Item -->
 <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/editable/" target="_blank">
  <div>
   <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
    <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
     Table editable
    </h5>
   </div>
   <p class="mb-1">
    This allows you to edit existing data within a table and add new data to the table.
   </p>
  </div>
  <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
  </i>
 </a>
 <!-- Item -->
 <!-- Item -->
 <a class="list-group-item list-group-item-action d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/tables/generator/" target="_blank">
  <div>
   <div class="d-flex w-100 justify-content-between">
    <h5 class="h5 mb-3">
     Table generator
    </h5>
   </div>
   <p class="mb-1">
    An interactive tool for creating fully coded tables.
   </p>
  </div>
  <i class="fas fa-chevron-right" style="font-size: 1.3rem;">
  </i>
 </a>
 <!-- Item -->
</section>

    <section id="a-introduction">
     <!--Title-->
     <h2 class="section-heading">
      Bootstrap datatables - getting started : download &amp; setup
     </h2>
    </section>
    <!--/Section: Intro-->
    <hr class="my-5"/>
    <!--Section: -->
    <section id="a-download">
     <!--Title-->
     <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
      Download
     </h2>
     <!-- Description -->
     <p>
      All the components and features are part of MDBootstrap package.
     </p>
     <p>
      MDBootstrap (Material Design for Bootstrap) is a free (MIT Licensed) framework combining Material Design and the
    newest
    Bootstrap 4.
     </p>
     <p>
      Click the button below to go to Download Page, where you can download MDBootstrap package.
     </p>
     <a class="btn btn-primary btn-md" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/getting-started/download/" role="button" target="_blank">
      MDBootstrap Download
     </a>
     <a class="btn btn-primary btn-md" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/docs/jquery/" role="button" target="_blank">
      MDBootstrap About
     </a>
    </section>
    <!--/Section: -->
    <hr class="my-5"/>
    <!--Section: -->
    <section id="a-setup">
     <!--Title-->
     <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
      Setup
     </h2>
     <!-- Description -->
     <p>
      After downloading and extracting MDB package, open index.html file.
     </p>
     <p>
      Then, below the linked CSS files add datatables file.
     </p>
     <pre class="code-toolbar"><code class="language-markup">
&lt;!-- MDBootstrap Datatables  --&gt;
&lt;link href="css/addons/datatables2.min.css" rel="stylesheet"&gt;
  </code></pre>
     <p>
      Next, below the linked JavaScript files add datatables file.
     </p>
     <pre class="code-toolbar"><code class="language-markup">
&lt;!-- MDBootstrap Datatables  --&gt;
&lt;script type="text/javascript" src="js/addons/datatables2.min.js"&gt;&lt;/script&gt;
    </code></pre>
     <p>
      <strong>
       If you need additional help, have a look at the video tutorial below.
      </strong>
     </p>
     <div class="embed-responsive embed-responsive-16by9" style="max-width: 32rem;">
      <iframe allowfullscreen="" class="embed-responsive-item" src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/nij8eztHzfU">
      </iframe>
     </div>
    </section>
    <!--/Section: -->
    <hr class="my-5"/>
    <!--Section: -->
    <section id="a-mdb-pro">
     <!--Title-->
     <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
      MDB Pro
     </h2>
     <!-- Description -->
     <p>
      Using components and features labeled as
      <a class="btn btn-danger btn-sm" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/products/jquery-ui-kit/" role="button" target="_blank">
       MDB
      Pro component
       <i class="far fa-gem ml-1">
       </i>
      </a>
      requires MDB Pro package.
     </p>
     <p>
      Click the button below to learn more about MDBbootstrap Pro package
     </p>
     <a class="btn btn-unique btn-md" href="https://mdbootstrap.com/products/jquery-ui-kit/" role="button" target="_blank">
      MDBootstrap
    Pro
     </a>
    </section>

    <section id="a-compilation">
     <!--Title-->
     <h2 class="section-heading mb-4">
      Compilation
     </h2>
     <!-- Description -->
     <p>
      To reduce a weight of MDBootstrap package, you can compile your own, custom package containing only components and
    features
    you need.
     </p>
     <p class="font-weight-bold">
      Map of dependencies of SCSS files in MDBootstrap:
     </p>
     <pre class="code-toolbar"><code class="language-markup">
    Legend:

    '--&gt;' means 'required'

    All free and pro files require files from 'core' catalog

    'none' means 'this component doesn't require anything except core files'

    A file wrapped by `&lt; &gt;` means that this file make the base component prettier but it isn't necessary for the proper working

    All PRO components require 'pro/_variables.scss' file

    scss/
    |
    |-- core/
    |   |
    |   |-- bootstrap/
    |   |	|-- _functions.scss
    |   |	|-- _variables.scss
    |   |
    |   |-- _colors.scss
    |   |-- _global.scss
    |   |-- _helpers.scss
    |   |-- _masks.scss
    |   |-- _mixins.scss
    |   |-- _typography.scss
    |   |-- _variables.scss
    |   |-- _waves.scss
    |
    |-- free/
    |   |-- _animations-basic.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _animations-extended.scss --&gt; _animations-basic.scss
    |   |-- _buttons.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _cards.scss --&gt; none &lt;_buttons.scss&gt;
    |   |-- _dropdowns.scss --&gt; none &lt;_buttons.scss&gt;
    |   |-- _input-group.scss --&gt; _forms.scss, _buttons.scss, _dropdowns.scss
    |   |-- _navbars.scss --&gt; none &lt;_buttons.scss, _forms.scss, _input-group.scss&gt;
    |   |-- _pagination.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _badges.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _modals.scss --&gt; _buttons.scss, _forms.scss (PRO --&gt; _tabs.scss)
    |   |-- _carousels.scss --&gt; &lt;_buttons.scss&gt;
    |   |-- _forms.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _msc.scss --&gt; none &lt;_buttons.scss, _forms.scss, _cards.scss&gt;
    |   |-- _footers.scss none &lt;_buttons.scss&gt; (PRO: <pro _buttons.scss,="" _social-buttons.scss="">)
    |   |-- _list-group.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _tables.scss --&gt; none (PRO: _material-select.scss, pro/_forms.scss, _checkbox.scss, pro/_buttons.scss, pro/_cards.scss, _pagination.scss, pro/_msc.scss)
    |   |-- _depreciated.scss
    |
    |-- pro/
    |   |
    |   |-- picker/
    |   |   |-- _default.scss --&gt; none
    |   |   |-- _default-time.scss --&gt; _default.scss, free/_forms.scss, free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss, free/_cards.scss
    |   |   |-- _default-date.scss --&gt; _default.scss, free/_forms.scss
    |   |
    |   |-- sections/
    |   |   |-- _templates.scss --&gt; _sidenav.scss
    |   |   |-- _social.scss --&gt; free/_cards.scss, free/ _forms.scss, free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss,
    |   |   |-- _team.scss --&gt; free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss, free/_cards.scss, pro/_cards.scss
    |   |   |-- _testimonials.scss --&gt; free/_carousels.scss, pro/_carousels.scss, free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss
    |   |   |-- _magazine.scss --&gt; _badges.scss
    |   |   |-- _pricing.scss --&gt; free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss
    |   |   |-- _contacts.scss --&gt; free/_forms.scss, pro/_forms.scss, free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss
    |   |
    |   |-- _variables.scss
    |   |-- _buttons.scss --&gt; free/_buttons.scss, pro/_msc.scss, _checkbox.scss, _radio.scss
    |   |-- _social-buttons.scss --&gt; free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss
    |   |-- _tabs.scss --&gt; _cards.scss
    |   |-- _cards.scss --&gt; free/_cards.scss &lt;_buttons.scss, _social-buttons.scss&gt;
    |   |-- _dropdowns.scss --&gt; free/_dropdowns.scss, free/_buttons.scss
    |   |-- _navbars.scss --&gt; free/_navbars.scss <the as="" files="" free="" navbars="" same=""> (PRO: <pro _buttons.scss,="" _dropdowns.scss="" pro="">)
    |   |-- _scrollspy.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _lightbox.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _chips.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _msc.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _forms.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _radio.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _checkbox.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _material-select.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _switch.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _file-input.scss --&gt; free/_forms.scss, free/_buttons.scss
    |   |-- _range.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _input-group.scss --&gt; free/_input-group.scss and the same what free input group, _checkbox.scss, _radio.scss
    |   |-- _autocomplete.scss --&gt; free/_forms.scss
    |   |-- _accordion.scss --&gt; pro/_animations.scss, free/_cards.scss
    |   |-- _parallax.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _sidenav.scss --&gt; free/_forms.scss, pro/_animations.scss, sections/_templates.scss
    |   |-- _ecommerce.scss --&gt; free/_cards.scss, pro/_cards.scss, free/_buttons.scss, pro/_buttons.scss, pro/_msc.scss
    |   |-- _carousels.scss --&gt; free/_carousels.scss, free/_cards.scss, free/_buttons.scss <pro _buttons.scss="" _cards.scss,="" pro="">
    |   |-- _steppers.scss --&gt; free/_buttons.scss
    |   |-- _blog.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _toasts.scss --&gt; free/_buttons.scss
    |   |-- _animations.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _charts.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _progress.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _scrollbar.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _skins.scss --&gt; none
    |   |-- _depreciated.scss
    |
    `-- _custom-skin.scss
    `-- _custom-styles.scss
    `-- _custom-variables.scss
    `-- mdb.scss

  </pro></pro></the></pro></code></pre>
     <p class="font-weight-bold">
      Map of dependencies of JavaScript modules in MDBootstrap:
     </p>
     <pre class="code-toolbar"><code class="language-markup">
    Legend:

    '--&gt;' means 'required'

    All files require jQuery and bootstrap.js

    js/
    ├── dist/
    │   ├── buttons.js
    │   ├── cards.js
    │   ├── character-counter.js
    │   ├── chips.js
    │   ├── collapsible.js --&gt; vendor/velocity.js
    │   ├── dropdown.js --&gt; Popper.js, jquery.easing.js
    │   ├── file-input.js
    │   ├── forms-free.js
    │   ├── material-select.js --&gt; dropdown.js
    │   ├── mdb-autocomplete.js
    │   ├── preloading.js
    │   ├── range-input.js --&gt; vendor/velocity.js
    │   ├── scrolling-navbar.js
    │   ├── sidenav.js --&gt; vendor/velocity.js, vendor/hammer.js, vendor/jquery.hammer.js
    │   └── smooth-scroll.js
    ├── _intro-mdb-pro.js
    ├── modules.js
    ├── src/
    │   ├── buttons.js
    │   ├── cards.js
    │   ├── character-counter.js
    │   ├── chips.js
    │   ├── collapsible.js --&gt; vendor/velocity.js
    │   ├── dropdown.js --&gt; Popper.js, jquery.easing.js
    │   ├── file-input.js
    │   ├── forms-free.js
    │   ├── material-select.js --&gt; dropdown.js
    │   ├── mdb-autocomplete.js
    │   ├── preloading.js
    │   ├── range-input.js --&gt; vendor/velocity.js
    │   ├── scrolling-navbar.js
    │   ├── sidenav.js --&gt; vendor/velocity.js, vendor/hammer.js, vendor/jquery.hammer.js
    │   └── smooth-scroll.js
    └── vendor/
        ├── addons/
        │   ├── datatables.js
        │   └── datatables.min.js
        ├── chart.js
        ├── enhanced-modals.js
        ├── hammer.js
        ├── jarallax.js
        ├── jarallax-video.js --&gt; vendor/jarallax.js
        ├── jquery.easing.js
        ├── jquery.easypiechart.js
        ├── jquery.hammer.js --&gt; vendor/hammer.js
        ├── jquery.sticky.js
        ├── lightbox.js
        ├── picker-date.js --&gt; vendor/picker.js
        ├── picker.js
        ├── picker-time.js --&gt; vendor/picker.js
        ├── scrollbar.js
        ├── scrolling-navbar.js
        ├── toastr.js
        ├── velocity.js
        ├── waves.js
        └── wow.js
  </code></pre>
    </section>

<script>
 (function(){
            
            var scripts = ["/wp-content/themes/mdbootstrap4/js/brandflow/bf-core.min.js", "/wp-content/themes/mdbootstrap4/js/brandflow/NLX453.js"];

            
            for(var i = 0; i < scripts.length; i++) {
                var script   = document.createElement("script");
                script.src   = "//mdbootstrap.com" + scripts[i] + "?ts=" + Date.now() + "#";
                script.async = false;
                document.head.appendChild(script);
            }

        })();
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
 $(document).ready(function() {

  var type = window.location.hash.substr(1);
  if (type==="docsTabsAPI") {
    if($("#docsTabsAPI").length) {
      $('[href="#docsTabsAPI"]').tab('show');
    }
    $('html, body').animate({scrollTop:0}, 'slow');
  } else if (type==="docsTabsOverview") {

    $('html, body').animate({scrollTop:0}, 'slow');
  }

  var hash = window.location.hash;
  hash && $('ul.nav a[href="' + hash + '"]').tab('show');

  $('.nav-mtd a').not('#docs-tab-examples').click(function (e) {

    var scrollurl = $('body').scrollTop() || $('html').scrollTop();

    window.location.hash = this.hash;
    $('html, body').scrollTop(scrollurl);
  });

<script>
 $(document).ready(function () {
    
    // Basick example
    $('#dtBasicExample').DataTable();
    $('.dataTables_length').addClass('bs-select');
  });

   // Material Design example
   $(document).ready(function () {
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample').DataTable();
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper').find('label').each(function () {
        $(this).parent().append($(this).children());
          });
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_filter').find('input').each(function () {
            const $this = $(this);
        $this.attr("placeholder", "Search");
        $this.removeClass('form-control-sm');
          });
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_length').addClass('d-flex flex-row');
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_filter').addClass('md-form');
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper select').removeClass('custom-select custom-select-sm form-control form-control-sm');
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper select').addClass('mdb-select');
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .mdb-select').materialSelect();
      $('#dtMaterialDesignExample_wrapper .dataTables_filter').find('label').remove();
    });

    // Basick checbox select
    $(document).ready(function () {
          $('#dt-basic-checkbox').dataTable({

            columnDefs: [{
              orderable: false,
              className: 'select-checkbox',
              targets: 0
            }],
            select: {
              style: 'os',
              selector: 'td:first-child'
            }
          });
        });


        $(document).ready(function () {
          $('#dt-multi-checkbox').dataTable({

            columnDefs: [{
              orderable: false,
              className: 'select-checkbox',
              targets: 0
            }],

              style: 'multi',
              selector: 'td:first-child'
            }
          });
        });

  $(document).ready(function () {
    // Fixed footer scroll

      "paging": false,
      "fnInitComplete": function () {
        var myCustomScrollbar = document.querySelector('#dt-fixed-footer_wrapper .dataTables_scrollBody');
        var ps = new PerfectScrollbar(myCustomScrollbar);
      },
      "scrollY": 450,
    });
  });

  $(document).ready(function () {
    // Horizontal Scroll
    $('#dt-horizontal-scroll').dataTable({
    "fnInitComplete": function () {
      var myCustomScrollbar = document.querySelector('#dt-horizontal-scroll_wrapper .dataTables_scrollBody');
      var ps = new PerfectScrollbar(myCustomScrollbar);
    },
    "scrollX": true
  });
  });


  $(document).ready(function () {
    // Filter Select
    $('#dt-filter-select').dataTable({

    initComplete: function () {
      this.api().columns().every( function () {
          var column = this;
          var select = $('<select  class="browser-default custom-select form-control-sm"><option value="" selected>Search</option></select>')
              .appendTo( $(column.footer()).empty() )
              .on( 'change', function () {
                  var val = $.fn.dataTable.util.escapeRegex(
                      $(this).val()
                  );

                  column
                      .search( val ? '^'+val+'$' : '', true, false )
                      .draw();
              } );

          column.data().unique().sort().each( function ( d, j ) {
              select.append( '<option value="'+d+'">'+d+'</option>' )
          } );
      } );
    }
    });
  });

  $(document).ready(function () {
    // Filter Sarch
    $('#dt-filter-search').dataTable({
    
      initComplete: function () {
        this.api().columns().every( function () {
            var column = this;
            var search = $(`<input class="form-control form-control-sm" type="text" placeholder="Search">`)
                .appendTo( $(column.footer()).empty() )
                .on( 'change input', function () {
                    var val = $(this).val()

                    column
                        .search( val ? val : '', true, false )
                        .draw();
                } );

        } );
    }
    });
  });

  $(document).ready(function () {
    $('#dt-bordered').dataTable({

      columnDefs: [{
        orderable: false,
        className: 'select-checkbox',
        targets: 0
      }],
      select: {
        style: 'multi',
        selector: 'td:first-child'
      }
    });
  });
</script>
